< Review>
The staff are great. We enjoying going in there cuz the staff are so helpful & curtious. My son is in the Navy, & was coming home for Christmas, & I had no clue what to buy him.(& I don't play video games at all. The only thing I knew; that he had a PS4) The staff asked a few questions about him, that I did know the answers to, & they made a suggestion of a game he might like. (Also letting me know I could return it if he didn't like it!!) My son came home, opened his gift, & LOVED the game!! The staff also let me know what was about to expire, via the points we had  earned, which really helped cuz it got me my sons game free, plus a huge discount on all the other items I was buying. I really appreciate the staffs help w/ this cuz as a mother, I just wanna see that smile of their faces, when you know you picked the right gift. They helped make that happen, for me & many others. I just can't give this store, & its staff, high enough marks. Thanks.< /Review>

<rate>5<//rate>< Text>
I absolutely love Gold Coast and their staff!!!!

I first learned of the car service back in November 2016, from a colleague who recommended them for taking me to the airport for business travel.

I have not strayed since.

I refuse to use an uber or lyft simply because of the impeccable service Mike and his team provides. I love their SUVs, usually Tahoe sized and above. Always clean inside, and it smells amazing!

Whoever comes to pick you up from home/airport will help you with your bags, which I truly appreciate as I am not as physically capable as I used to be in my youth.

The staff appearance is professional, usually in either a full suit or business casual -- more on the business side. Their attitudes and friendliness go a long way. I appreciate every ride they have ever given me.

You can't go wrong with Gold Coast. They have never left me stranded, no matter what time of the day I need to be picked up. I think the latest/earliest time once was when I arrived into San Diego at 3:00 AM! Mike always makes sure that either he or another one of his drivers is there to take you home safely.

If for whatever reason, the driver gets held up, they will let you know and communicate it to you ASAP via text or phone call. One time a driver of mine got held up by traffic. No big deal, I was able to kill time by smoking a cigarette and stretching my legs after a long flight.

They are very accommodating to the fact that stuff happens! If your flight gets delayed, just text Mike ASAP and he will make sure that there is someone there to get you.

5 stars to Mike and his team. You guys are awesome!< /Text>

< Review>
Proshop Automotive is cutting edge. The technology they use is incredibly impressive. Plus, there is a check-in system that prompts and email with a link to your car's service record. There, you can view recommendations, see photos of the problems the technicians find, and you can approve or deny any work (and see all estimates) before you find yourself stuck with sticker shock. These guys are thorough and super polite and friendly. If you have questions, they take the time to answer them. I'm a repeat customer and will continue to be their customer in the future. They make car repairs as painless as possible. Plus, if you are within 10 miles of the shop, they will come pick up your vehicle and bring it back to you when the work is done. Each time they have worked on my car, they even bring it back washed and shiny - inside and out. I hate having my car serviced. HATE IT! However, the great folks over at Proshop Automotive make it so easy and painless that it's actually kinda fun! I sincerely appreciate the photos they post with any of their findings. That helps you see that you're not being snowed over. There is never any pressure to do any of the work they recommend. They're just as polite to you if you tell them to do it all as they are if you decline all the recommendations. Super fun bunch! Superior customer service! Excellent repair work. < review>
Don't let the location drive you away from this gem. The area seems a bit sketchy but man is it worth it. The bakery itself has some of the best pastries I have ever tasted, not over sweet or over produced.

At night there is a taco truck out front which toes just T.J. style tacos. I had the chorizo, adobado, and asada,  each were juicy flavorful and filling. You get your money's worth at this place.</review>

< Review>
This place gets all 5 stars for the great food, coffee, and you cant leave without getting some pan. They also have cheesecake and smoothies. Everything is good. We came to try thier tortas and they surpassed expectations. We had the torta chilanga and torta cubana. Full of flavor from your ordinary torta. Highly recommend it. It comes with a side of fries. Service is so-so.
Waited in line while cashiers counted their cash. Never before been to a store where both registers counted cash while customers were waiting. We also had to clean our own table.

Good selection of sweet delights and everything looks good.
We had the Tres Leches (vanilla). Ours was a little too moist and the bottom consisted of a thin chocolate crust which I think detracted from the overall flavour. It was okay but there are better to be found in San Diego. Barra Barra Saloon in Old Towne (San Diego) is better.

Better yet,  make the 7 hour drive to Seaside, CA., and have the absolute best Tres Leches in California at La Tortuga Restaurant. Yeah, I know, it's a long drive. Do you want the best or don't you?</text>
